***метнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:метнуть.html>метну́ть</a> (11391)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ну́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метнуть.html>метну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">metnútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw, to cast, to fling
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:метнуть.html>метну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:диск.html>диск</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>metnútʹ</b> disk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw the discus</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:метнуть.html>метну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:копье.html>копьё</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>metnútʹ</b> kopʹjó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to throw the javelin</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:метнуть.html>метну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жребий.html>жре́бий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>metnútʹ</b> žrébij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">cast lots</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>A rare and awkward past passive participle <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">мётнутый</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mjótnutyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is occasionally found.
</p>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i>See <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for derived verbs.</i></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">мета́тель</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">metátelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метательный.html>мета́тельный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">metátelʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:мета.html>ме́т</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ну́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:совершённый.html>совершенный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:переходный.html>перехо́дный</a>,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 3b.      <a href = vnd.unilang:соответствующий.html>Соотве́тствующий</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>глаго́л</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нного</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>ви́да</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a>.
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:производный.html>Произво́дное</a>: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></b> ➔ <a href = vnd.unilang:мета.html>ме́т</a> + <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ну.html>ну</a></b> + ть (суффиксальный).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мет-</b>; суффикс: <b>-ну</b>; глагольное <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ть</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*měxъ</i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:механический.html>механи́ческий</a> (4738)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">меха́н(ика)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mexán(ika)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:механический.html>механи́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mexaníčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>mechanical <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">related to mechanics; done by machine</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>automatic <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">acting without conscious thought</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́ченный</a> (15748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́ченный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">méčennyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past passive imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<hr><hr><h3><span id=".D0.9C.D0.BE.D1.80.D1.84.D0.BE.D0.BB.D0.BE.D0.B3.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D0.B8_.D1.81.D0.B8.D0.BD.D1.82.D0.B0.D0.BA.D1.81.D0.B8.D1.87.D0.B5.D1.81.D0.BA.D0.B8.D0.B5_.D1.81.D0.B2.D0.BE.D0.B9.D1.81.D1.82.D0.B2.D0.B0"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Морфологические_и_синтаксические_свойства"></span></h3>

<p><b>ме́<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>чен<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>ный</b>
</p><p>Страдательное <a href = vnd.unilang:причастие.html>прича́стие</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:прошедший.html>проше́дшего</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мени</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1*a(2).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-меч-</b>; суффикс: <b>-енн</b>; <a href = vnd.unilang:окончание.html>оконча́ние</a>: <b>-ый</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.
</p>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-еный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-enyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меченый.html>ме́ченый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">méčenyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>marked, labeled, tagged</li></ol>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Short forms <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меченный.html>ме́чен</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:меченный.html>ме́чена</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:меченный.html>ме́чено</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:меченный.html>ме́чены</a></span> theoretically exist, but are usually avoided, as they are the same as the short forms of the past passive participle of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́тить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">métitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***мечеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечеть.html>мече́ть</a> (18168)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> language (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kazakh_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kazakh language">Kazakh</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="kk">мешіт</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="kk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">meşit</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Tatar_language" class="extiw" title="w:Tatar language">Tatar</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="tt">мәчет</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="tt-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mäçet</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkmen_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkmen language">Turkmen</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tk">metjit</i>), ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Arabic" class="extiw" title="w:Arabic">Arabic</a></span> <i class="Arab mention" lang="ar">مَسْجِد</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ar-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">masjid</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечеть.html>мече́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mečétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечеть.html>мече́ти</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечеть.html>мече́ти</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечеть.html>мече́тей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>mosque</li></ol>

<p><b>ме<span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span>че́ть</b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:существительное.html>Существи́тельное</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:неодушевленный.html>неодушевлённое</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:женский.html>же́нский</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:род.html>род</a>, 3-е <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ние</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:склонение.html>склоне́ния</a> 8a  <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка).
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:корень.html>Ко́рень</a>: <b>-мечеть-</b> <sup> | Тихонов, 1996 | </sup>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечтание.html>мечта́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mečtánije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечтание.html>мечта́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечтание.html>мечта́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечта.html>мечта́ний</a></b>)

***мечтать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:мечтать.html>мечта́ть</a> (1434)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mьčьtati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:мечтать.html>мечта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mečtátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:помечтать.html>помечта́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dream</li></ol>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:меч.html>меч</a><span class="hyph" style="color:lightgreen;">-</span><a href = vnd.unilang:тать.html>та́ть</a></b>
</p><p><a href = vnd.unilang:глагол.html>Глаго́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:несовершенный.html>несоверше́нный</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вид.html>вид</a>, непереходный,    <a href = vnd.unilang:тип.html>тип</a> спряжения <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:классификация.html>классифика́ции</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a>. Зализняка — 1a. <a href = vnd.unilang:участник.html>Уча́стники</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ции</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:описываемый.html>опи́сываемой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:помощь.html>по́мощью</a> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:мечтать.html>мечта́ть</a></i>: <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/3f/NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-1.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:субъект.html>субъект</a> (им.), <img alt="NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/24px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png" decoding="async" width="24" height="24" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/36px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/61/NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg/48px-NYCS-bull-trans-2.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="75" data-file-height="75" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:предмет.html>предме́т</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:желание.html>жела́ний</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> + пр.).
